***сбить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сбить.html>сбить</a> (2607)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бить.html>бить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбить.html>сби́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sbítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбивать.html>сбива́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to knock down</li>
<li>to cause to fall, to shake down
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбить.html>сбить</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:спесь.html>спесь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> кого́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sbitʹ spesʹ s kovó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to take smb. down a peg, to cut smb. down to size</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбить.html>сбить</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:цена.html>це́ну</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sbitʹ cénu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to beat down the price</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to put out
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбить.html>сбить</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>та́кта</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sbitʹ s tákta</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put out of time</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбить.html>сбить</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:со.html>со</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:след.html>сле́да</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sbitʹ so sléda</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put off the scent</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбить.html>сбить</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:толк.html>толку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sbitʹ s tolku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to bewilder, to confuse, to muddle</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбить.html>сбить</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:путь.html>пути́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:истинный.html>и́стинного</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sbitʹ s putí ístinnovo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to lead astray</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to tread down</li>
<li>to knock together</li>
<li>to churn</li>
<li><i>(eggs, cream)</i> to whisk, to beat, to whip</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сбиться.html>сби́ться</a> (5616)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбить.html>сбить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sbitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбиться.html>сби́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sbítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбиваться.html>сбива́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to get off</li>
<li>to be aberrant</li>
<li>to go afield</li>
<li>to go astray</li>
<li>to be errant, to stray</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбить.html>сбить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sbitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сближаться.html>сближа́ться</a> (21204)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сближать.html>сближа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sbližátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сближаться.html>сближа́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sbližátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сблизиться.html>сбли́зиться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to approach <i>(each other)</i></li>
<li>to approach, to close in</li>
<li>to draw closer together</li>
<li>to become good/close friends <i>(with)</i></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сближать.html>сближа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sbližátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***сблизиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сблизиться.html>сбли́зиться</a> (17470)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сблизить.html>сбли́зить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sblízitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сблизиться.html>сбли́зиться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sblízitʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сближаться.html>сближа́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to approach <i>(each other)</i></li>
<li>to approach, to close in</li>
<li>to draw closer together
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наш.html>на́ши</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:точка.html>то́чки</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:зрение.html>зре́ния</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сблизиться.html>сбли́зились</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">náši tóčki zrénija <b>sblízilisʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">our points of view have drawn nearer; we are beginning to understand each other's point of view</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to become good/close friends <i>(with)</i></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сблизить.html>сбли́зить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sblízitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сбой.html>сбой</a> (12848)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбой.html>сбой</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sboj</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбой.html>сбо́я</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбой.html>сбо́и</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбой.html>сбои́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбой.html>сбо́ев</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбой.html>сбоёв</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>failure, fault, error

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sports</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> losing the step, falling out of step</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сболтнуть.html>сболтну́ть</a> (21729)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сболтнуть.html>сболтну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sboltnútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to just happen to say something, to say something silly (or wrong), to blurt out

***сбор.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сбор.html>сбор</a> (2955)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">съборъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sŭborŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:собор.html>собо́р</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sobór</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, borrowed from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span></span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбор.html>сбор</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sbor</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбор.html>сбо́ра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбор.html>сбо́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбор.html>сбо́ров</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>collection, accumulation, gathering, harvest, picking</li>
<li>levy, tax, duty, receipts</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> muster, assembly</li>
<li>assembly, meeting, get-together</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:собирание.html>собира́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sobiránije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:урожай.html>урожа́й</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">urožáj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***сборка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сборка.html>сбо́рка</a> (14411)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbal of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:собрать.html>собра́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sobrátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, based on the nominal combining stem <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">сбор-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sbor-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, derived from the present tense stem <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">сбер-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sber-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> with Indo-European <i>o</i>-vocalization characteristic of deverbal nouns.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сборка.html>сбо́рка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sbórka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сборка.html>сбо́рки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сборка.html>сбо́рки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сборка.html>сбо́рок</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">сбо́рочный</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>assembly <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">e.g. of devices or machines</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">секцио́нная <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сборка.html>сбо́рка</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sekciónnaja <b>sbórka</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">sectional/unit assembly</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:графика.html>гра́фик</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сборка.html>сбо́рки</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">gráfik <b>sbórki</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">assembly schedule</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>pleat</li></ol>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">engineering</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> storage tank, receptacle</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сборщик.html>сбо́рщик</a> (21607)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбор.html>сбор</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sbor</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-щик</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ščik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбросить.html>сбро́сить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sbrósitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбрасывать.html>сбра́сывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sbrásyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбросить.html>сбро́сить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to throw down, to drop</li>
<li><i>(a government)</i> to throw off</li>
<li><i>(skin, leaves)</i> to shed</li>
<li><i>(clothes, shoes)</i> to throw off</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сброд.html>сброд</a> (21689)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сброд.html>сброд</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sbrod</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сброд.html>сбро́да</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сброс.html>сброс</a> (30987)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbal of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбросить.html>сбро́сить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sbrósitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сброс.html>сброс</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sbros</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сброс.html>сбро́са</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сброс.html>сбро́сы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сброс.html>сбро́сов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>water escape</li>
<li>dumping, discharge
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сброс.html>сброс</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сточный.html>сто́чных</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вода.html>вод</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sbros</b> stóčnyx vod</i> ― <span class="e-translation">dumping/discharge of sewage</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сброс.html>сброс</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:отход.html>отхо́дов</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:море.html>мо́ре</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sbros</b> otxódov v móre</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sea dumping/burial of waste</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>reduction, dropping
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сброс.html>сброс</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:давление.html>давле́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sbros</b> davlénija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">pressure release/relief/drop</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сброс.html>сброс</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:нагрузка.html>нагру́зки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sbros</b> nagrúzki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">load relief/shedding</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">computer science</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> reset, resetting, clearance, nulling, nullification, zeroing</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">geology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> fault</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сбросить.html>сбро́сить</a> (2789)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бросить.html>бро́сить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">brósitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбросить.html>сбро́сить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sbrósitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбрасывать.html>сбра́сывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to throw down, to drop</li>
<li><i>(a government)</i> to throw off</li>
<li><i>(skin, leaves)</i> to shed</li>
<li><i>(clothes, shoes)</i> to throw off</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбывать.html>сбыва́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sbyvátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбыть.html>сбы́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to sell, to market</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to get rid of</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сбыт.html>сбыт</a> (13557)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbal from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбыть.html>сбыть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sbytʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбыт.html>сбыт</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sbyt</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сбыт.html>сбы́та</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li class="senseid" id="Russian-sale">sale
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:рынок.html>ры́нок</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сбыт.html>сбы́та</a></b></i></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><i>rýnok <b>sbýta</b></i></i> ― <span class="e-translation">(seller's) market</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сбыт.html>сбыт</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:наркотик.html>нарко́тиков</a></i></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><i><b>sbyt</b> narkotikov</i></i> ― <span class="e-translation">drug industry</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
